####  Piano-Forest  
##### 3#         楼主| 发表于 2022-8-23 08:24

今年设立的新奖项：

“最佳改编”（游戏IP相关衍生作品，比如改编为电影、书籍以及漫画之类的）

This year @TheGameAwards introduces a new category:

<strong>BEST ADAPTATION</strong> to recognize outstanding work adapting video game IP to other entertainment forms.

We will celebrate shows, movies, books, podcasts, comics + more that authentically adapt the source material. 

*****

####  Piano-Forest  
##### 4#         楼主| 发表于 2022-9-21 09:10

“Future Class”设立的第三年（该奖项旨在庆祝我们光明的、大胆的、具有包容性的游戏的未来）

玩家可以前往网站填写表单，提名那些在游戏中提供多元化服务的个人，包括游戏内容创作者、电竞选手和游戏界从业人士等
<img src="https://p.sda1.dev/7/ba6bfabfa0656903771e8916fffd4cee/20220921_090722.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

提名地址，截止至10月21日（需谷歌账号）：
[https://docs.google.com/forms/d/ ... SWDxgEa8WA/viewform](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSdbNj0DOO75rmqzTuZXsG9uNutQB7APTDeAn21XSWDxgEa8WA/viewform)

去年的最终结果名单：
[https://thegameawards.com/future-class](https://thegameawards.com/future-class)

This new AAA project is an character-based, online, third-person action game, set in a new and original world.

[https://twitter.com/AirshipSyn/status/1575530854801149954](https://twitter.com/AirshipSyn/status/1575530854801149954)

Skylight isn’t just the codename of our next adventure… it’s also the name of the main city in the game. Skylight is the last bastion of hope for humanity and a place you’ll call home.

Here is what it looks like in-game.

约瑟夫·法尔斯（双人成行 制作人）将为今年的年度游戏颁奖

谈及新作（并未说到是否会在今年TGA上公开）：

“We’re so focussed on the next game… I can’t say it’s only one [Ievel], but I’m still looking back on it now thinking ‘this is a fucking good game’[Laughs]”.

“Get ready for me man, I’m coming. Trust me… it will blow your fucking mind.” 

it will be a "surprise in a good way"

"And it’ll be something really fucking cool.”

我就很喜欢stray，今年唯二白金的游戏，你说游戏设计差，表达差。我也不觉得差到那里，美术风格，关卡设计，情感表达，世界观设定都戳我心头。唯一差的在我看来反而是猫猫的塑造，作为爱猫人士而言我觉得还是很拉胯。

今年5个indie我都有玩过。唯一没玩下去的就是tunic，让我选择的话，我会选光之传说，神之天平，stray，sifu和吸血鬼生存。我最喜欢的是光之传说，玩得最久的是吸血鬼，最令我佩服的是神之天平，但年度我会给sifu。

每个人心中的爱好就行了，抱怨抱怨发个两三楼楼也就算了，非要这么发癫表现自己的下限，反而连带让我对卡比的印象都变差了。

####  Piano-Forest  
##### 207#         楼主| 发表于 2022-11-27 22:15

杰夫：

40～50个游戏将参展（甚至可能会有小岛的新作）

我不想再承诺会有像12个Elden Ring之类的东西而惹上麻烦（艹，是去年的事吧<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face2017/068.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"> ）

但我们感觉很好，这将是我们更强大的阵容。你可能会在展会上看到10+新作

This year’s show promises a new category for the awards (bumping the total to 31 with the inclusion of Best Adaptation), <strong>glimpses of 40 to 50 games (a handful of which will be brand-new teasers), and perhaps even a showing of game dev auteur Hideo Kojima’s latest project </strong>(He is, showrunner Geoff Keighley points out, a “dear friend of the show.”)

As is always the case in the run-up to the show, Keighley was a bit cagey about what exactly to expect from this year’s show. 

What he did say was that The Game Awards would probably have 40 to 50 games across the show – some reveals, some existing titles. 

“It’s a strong year for us, for new game announcements for sure,” he added. “I don’t want to get in trouble by promising, like, 12 Elden Rings or something, but we feel good. This will be one of our stronger line-ups. <strong>There are probably more than a dozen new things you’ll see at the show.</strong>”

小岛方面的询问：

And what about Hideo Kojima? Kojima has a long history of collaborating with Keighley on reveals, is on the show’s advisory board, and was not too long ago teasing his new creation.

“No updates on Hideo’s status,” Keighley said. “<strong>But he is obviously a dear friend of the show. I'm sure he will participate in some way. </strong>I think he's still figuring out his plans. So I'm sure in some way he will play a role. I think we're still trying to figure out what he exactly is going to do.”

####  NeverCU

很多人没意识到一点：不是1人1票，而是1账号/邮箱1票，参考票的峰值1小时2000票。一个千人团体可以完成控票。这也是饭圈的恐怖之处。
目前来看还没有出现换票和海底捞的行为，只能说相比萌战，游戏圈投票还是太年轻了，门槛设置太低，不过为了热度可以理解。一但形成了稳定的饭圈，这种投票将被完全操控。

####  skdom  
##### 535#       发表于 2022-12-9 10:26

 本帖最后由 skdom 于 2022-12-9 10:28 编辑 
<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=58844047&amp;ptid=2088459" target="_blank">nage560 发表于 2022-12-9 10:15</a>

不是故事讲完了吗，还能出2？</blockquote>
续作这东西，其实很多种玩法

包括并不限于后日谈（主流）、前传（例如大镳客2就是1的前传）、与前作同时发生的另一组角色的故事、很多年后的故事（例如异度之刃2和3就是这种）、同世界观的另一个故事，甚至另一个世界线的故事也不是没有出现过

当然还有FF、DQ、传说、火纹这种只保留风格和一些代表性的物品的相互完全独立的所谓续作

此外还有石头门、混沌头、萝卜本，以及Never 7、Ever 17、Remember 11这种名字采用相同格式，但各不相同的系列续作
